<pr_description>
[Bug]: CKAN copies files infinitely if clone target folder is subdirectory of source folder
### Is there an existing issue for this?

- [x] I have checked the existing issues for an existing issue. I even actually looked at the ones that are pinned to the top!

### Operating System

Linux

### CKAN Version

v1.36.0

### Games

KSP 1

### Game Version

v1.24.5 or something

### Did you make any manual changes to your game folder (i.e., not via CKAN)?

_No response_

### Describe the bug

I tried to clone my default instance, Kerbal Space Program, to a new instance called RP1, and thought I would fit the new instance into a subdirectory of the original instance folder. It was taking a while so I left it and forgot about it, and lo and behold, I have 600 gigabytes of RP1 instance, due to CKAN repeatedly copying the files it copied into RP1 into itself.

CKAN should either detect when to not copy recursively, using some standard operating system copy tool that doesn't do this, or throw an error if the canonicalised path of the target folder is a subdirectory of the canonicalised path of the source directory.

<img width="1920" height="937" alt="Image" src="https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/50dadd96-b521-4c17-b25f-1d4934f1ea91" />

<img width="403" height="34" alt="Image" src="https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/a46f339c-ab59-41b4-bd39-cafca450bd0a" />

### Steps to reproduce

Clone an instance and set the target directory to a subdirectory of the original

     1	using System;
     2	using System.IO;
     3	using System.Linq;
     4	using System.Threading.Tasks;
     5	using System.ComponentModel;
     6	using System.Windows.Forms;
     7	#if NET5_0_OR_GREATER
     8	using System.Runtime.Versioning;
     9	#endif
    10	
    11	using Autofac;
    12	
    13	using CKAN.Games;
    14	using CKAN.IO;
    15	
    16	namespace CKAN.GUI
    17	{
    18	    /// <summary>
    19	    /// The GUI implementation of clone.
    20	    /// It's a separate window, handling the whole process.
    21	    /// </summary>
    22	    #if NET5_0_OR_GREATER
    23	    [SupportedOSPlatform("windows")]
    24	    #endif
    25	    public partial class CloneGameInstanceDialog : Form
    26	    {
    27	        private readonly GameInstanceManager manager;
    28	        private readonly IUser               user;
    29	
    30	        public CloneGameInstanceDialog(GameInstanceManager manager,
    31	                                       IUser               user,
    32	                                       string?             selectedInstanceName = null)
    33	            : base()
    34	        {
    35	            this.manager = manager;
    36	            this.user    = user;
    37	
    38	            InitializeComponent();
    39	
    40	            ToolTip.SetToolTip(checkBoxShareStock, Properties.Resources.CloneGameInstanceToolTipShareStock);
    41	
    42	            // Populate the instances combobox with names of known instances
    43	            comboBoxKnownInstance.DataSource =
    44	                Enumerable.Repeat("", 1)
    45	                          .Concat(manager.Instances.Values
    46	                                                   .Where(i => i.Valid)
    47	                                                   .OrderByDescending(i => i.Game.FirstReleaseDate)
    48	                                                   .ThenByDescending(i => i.Version())
    49	                                                   .ThenBy(i => i.Name)
    50	                                                   .Select(i => i.Name))
    51	                          .ToList();
    52	            comboBoxKnownInstance.Text = selectedInstanceName
    53	                                             ?? manager.CurrentInstance?.Name
    54	                                             ?? manager.Configuration.AutoStartInstance
    55	                                             ?? "";
    56	
    57	            if (Platform.IsWindows)
    58	            {
    59	                checkBoxShareStock.Checked = true;
    60	            }
    61	            else
    62	            {
    63	                // Symbolic links break cloned instances on Linux
    64	                // (Games use paths like <GameRoot>/KSP_Data/../saves/,
    65	                //  which follow the symlinks to the original instance)
    66	                checkBoxShareStock.Visible = false;
    67	            }
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        #region clone
    71	
    72	        private void comboBoxKnownInstance_SelectedIndexChanged(object? sender, EventArgs? e)
    73	        {
    74	            if (comboBoxKnownInstance.SelectedItem is string sel
    75	                && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(sel))
    76	            {
    77	                var inst = manager.Instances[sel];
    78	                textBoxClonePath.Text = Platform.FormatPath(inst.GameDir);
    79	                OptionalPathsListView.Items.Clear();
    80	                OptionalPathsListView.Items.AddRange(
    81	                    inst.Game.LeaveEmptyInClones
    82	                             .OrderBy(path => path,
    83	                                      StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
    84	                             .Select(path => new ListViewItem(path) { Tag = path })
    85	                             .ToArray());
    86	                OptionalPathsLabel.Visible = OptionalPathsListView.Visible =
    87	                    OptionalPathsListView.Items.Count > 0;
    88	            }
    89	        }
    90	
    91	        /// <summary>
    92	        /// Open an file dialog to search for a game instance, like in <code>ManageGameInstancesDialog</code>.
    93	        /// </summary>
    94	        private void buttonInstancePathSelection_Click(object? sender, EventArgs? e)
    95	        {
    96	            // Create a new FileDialog object
    97	            OpenFileDialog instanceDialog = new OpenFileDialog()
    98	            {
    99	                AddExtension     = false,
   100	                CheckFileExists  = false,
   101	                CheckPathExists  = false,
   102	                InitialDirectory = Environment.CurrentDirectory,
   103	                Filter           = ManageGameInstancesDialog.GameFolderFilter(),
   104	                Multiselect      = false
   105	            };
   106	
   107	            // Show the FileDialog and let the user search for the game directory.
   108	            if (instanceDialog.ShowDialog(this) != DialogResult.OK || !File.Exists(instanceDialog.FileName))
   109	            {
   110	                return;
   111	            }
   112	
   113	            // Write the path to the textbox
   114	            textBoxClonePath.Text = Path.GetDirectoryName(instanceDialog.FileName);
   115	        }
   116	
   117	        #endregion
   118	
   119	        /// <summary>
   120	        /// User is done. Start cloning or faking, depending on the clicked radio button.
   121	        /// Close the window if everything went right.
   122	        /// </summary>
   123	        private async void buttonOK_Click(object? sender, EventArgs? e)
   124	        {
   125	            string existingPath = textBoxClonePath.Text;
   126	            string newName = textBoxNewName.Text;
   127	            string newPath = textBoxNewPath.Text;
   128	
   129	            // Do some basic checks.
   130	            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(newName))
   131	            {
   132	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.CloneFakeKspDialogEnterName);
   133	                return;
   134	            }
   135	            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(newPath))
   136	            {
   137	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.CloneFakeKspDialogEnterPath);
   138	                return;
   139	            }
   140	
   141	            // Show progress bar and deactivate controls.
   142	            progressBar.Style = ProgressBarStyle.Marquee;
   143	            progressBar.Show();
   144	            foreach (Control ctrl in Controls)
   145	            {
   146	                ctrl.Enabled = false;
   147	            }
   148	
   149	            user.RaiseMessage(Properties.Resources.CloneFakeKspDialogCloningInstance);
   150	
   151	            try
   152	            {
   153	                var instanceToClone = comboBoxKnownInstance.SelectedItem is string s
   154	                                      && manager.Instances.TryGetValue(s, out GameInstance? instFromBox)
   155	                                      && existingPath == Platform.FormatPath(instFromBox.GameDir)
   156	                                          ? instFromBox
   157	                                          : manager.DetermineGame(new DirectoryInfo(existingPath), user) is IGame sourceGame
   158	                                              ? new GameInstance(sourceGame, existingPath,
   159	                                                                 "irrelevant", user)
   160	                                              : null;
   161	                if (instanceToClone == null)
   162	                {
   163	                    // User cancelled, let them try again
   164	                    reactivateDialog();
   165	                    return;
   166	                }
   167	                await Task.Run(() =>
   168	                {
   169	                    if (instanceToClone.Valid)
   170	                    {
   171	                        var cloned = manager.CloneInstance(instanceToClone, newName, newPath,
   172	                                                           OptionalPathsListView.Items
   173	                                                                                .OfType<ListViewItem>()
   174	                                                                                .Where(lvi => !lvi.Checked)
   175	                                                                                .Select(lvi => lvi.Tag)
   176	                                                                                .OfType<string>()
   177	                                                                                .ToArray(),
   178	                                                           checkBoxShareStock.Checked);
   179	                        var newGuiConfig = GUIConfiguration.LoadOrCreateConfiguration(instanceToClone, manager.SteamLibrary);
   180	                        // Don't clone Steam command lines
   181	                        newGuiConfig.CommandLines.RemoveAll(SteamLibrary.IsSteamCmdLine);
   182	                        newGuiConfig.Save(cloned);
   183	                    }
   184	                    else
   185	                    {
   186	                        throw new NotGameDirKraken(instanceToClone.GameDir);
   187	                    }
   188	                });
   189	
   190	                if (checkBoxSetAsDefault.Checked)
   191	                {
   192	                    manager.SetAutoStart(newName);
   193	                }
   194	
   195	                if (checkBoxSwitchInstance.Checked)
   196	                {
   197	                    manager.SetCurrentInstance(newName);
   198	                }
   199	
   200	                user.RaiseMessage(Properties.Resources.CloneFakeKspDialogSuccessfulClone);
   201	
   202	                DialogResult = DialogResult.OK;
   203	                Close();
   204	            }
   205	            catch (Kraken kraken)
   206	            {
   207	                user.RaiseError("{0}", kraken.Message);
   208	                reactivateDialog();
   209	            }
   210	            catch (Exception ex)
   211	            {
   212	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.CloneFakeKspDialogCloneFailed, ex.Message);
   213	                reactivateDialog();
   214	            }
   215	        }
   216	
   217	        private void buttonCancel_Click(object? sender, EventArgs? e)
   218	        {
   219	            DialogResult = DialogResult.Cancel;
   220	            Close();
   221	        }
   222	
   223	        /// <summary>
   224	        /// Activate all controls and hide progress bar.
   225	        /// </summary>
   226	        private void reactivateDialog()
   227	        {
   228	            foreach (Control ctrl in Controls)
   229	            {
   230	                ctrl.Enabled = true;
   231	            }
   232	            progressBar.Style = ProgressBarStyle.Continuous;
   233	            progressBar.Value = 0;
   234	            progressBar.Hide();
   235	        }
   236	
   237	        private void buttonPathBrowser_Click(object? sender, EventArgs? e)
   238	        {
   239	            if (folderBrowserDialogNewPath.ShowDialog(this).Equals(DialogResult.OK))
   240	            {
   241	                textBoxNewPath.Text = folderBrowserDialogNewPath.SelectedPath;
   242	            }
   243	        }
   244	
   245	        /// <summary>
   246	        /// Open the user guide when the user presses F1
   247	        /// </summary>
   248	        protected override void OnHelpRequested(HelpEventArgs evt)
   249	        {
   250	            evt.Handled = Util.TryOpenWebPage(HelpURLs.CloneFakeInstances);
   251	        }
   252	
   253	        /// <summary>
   254	        /// Open the user guide when the user clicks the help button
   255	        /// </summary>
   256	        protected override void OnHelpButtonClicked(CancelEventArgs evt)
   257	        {

   259	        }

   261	    }

    19	
    20	namespace CKAN
    21	{
    22	    /// <summary>
    23	    /// Manage multiple game installs.
    24	    /// </summary>
    25	    public class GameInstanceManager : IDisposable
    26	    {
    27	        /// <summary>
    28	        /// An IUser object for user interaction.
    29	        /// It is initialized during the startup with a ConsoleUser,
    30	        /// do not use in functions that could be called by the GUI.
    31	        /// </summary>
    32	        public IUser          User            { get; set; }
    33	        public IConfiguration Configuration   { get; set; }
    34	        public GameInstance?  CurrentInstance { get; private set; }
    35	        public event Action<GameInstance?, GameInstance?>? InstanceChanged;
    36	
    37	        public NetModuleCache? Cache { get; private set; }
    38	        public event Action<NetModuleCache>? CacheChanged;
    39	
    40	        public  SteamLibrary  SteamLibrary => steamLib ??= new SteamLibrary();
    41	        private SteamLibrary? steamLib;
    42	
    43	        private static readonly ILog log = LogManager.GetLogger(typeof (GameInstanceManager));
    44	
    45	        private readonly SortedList<string, GameInstance> instances = new SortedList<string, GameInstance>();
    46	
    47	        public SortedList<string, GameInstance> Instances => new SortedList<string, GameInstance>(instances);
    48	
    49	        public GameInstanceManager(IUser          user,
    50	                                   IConfiguration configuration,
    51	                                   SteamLibrary?  steamLib = null)
    52	        {
    53	            User = user;
    54	            Configuration = configuration;
    55	            this.steamLib = steamLib;
    56	            LoadInstances();
    57	            LoadCacheSettings();
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        /// <summary>
    61	        /// Returns the preferred game instance, or null if none can be found.
    62	        ///
    63	        /// This works by checking to see if we're in a game dir first, then the
    64	        /// config for an autostart instance, then will try to auto-populate
    65	        /// by scanning for the game.
    66	        ///
    67	        /// This *will not* touch the config if we find a portable install.
    68	        ///
    69	        /// This *will* run game instance autodetection if the config is empty.
    70	        ///
    71	        /// This *will* set the current instance, or throw an exception if it's already set.
    72	        ///
    73	        /// Returns null if we have multiple instances, but none of them are preferred.
    74	        /// </summary>
    75	        public GameInstance? GetPreferredInstance()
    76	            => CurrentInstance ??= _GetPreferredInstance();
    77	
    78	        private GameInstance? _GetPreferredInstance()
    79	        {
    80	            // First check if we're part of a portable install
    81	            // Note that this *does not* register in the config.
    82	            switch (KnownGames.knownGames.Select(g => GameInstance.PortableDir(g)
    83	                                                      is string p
    84	                                                          ? new GameInstance(g, p,
    85	                                                                             Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerPortable,
    86	                                                                             User)
    87	                                                          : null)
    88	                                         .OfType<GameInstance>()
    89	                                         .Where(i => i.Valid)
    90	                                         .ToArray())
    91	            {
    92	                case { Length: 1 } insts:
    93	                    return insts.Single();
    94	
    95	                case { Length: > 1 } insts:
    96	                    if (User.RaiseSelectionDialog(
    97	                            string.Format(Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerSelectGamePrompt,
    98	                                          string.Join(", ", insts.Select(i => i.GameDir)
    99	                                                                 .Distinct()
   100	                                                                 .Select(Platform.FormatPath))),
   101	                            insts.Select(i => i.Game.ShortName)
   102	                                 .ToArray())
   103	                        is int selection and >= 0)
   104	                    {
   105	                        return insts[selection];
   106	                    }
   107	                    break;
   108	            }
   109	
   110	            // If we only know of a single instance, return that.
   111	            if (instances.Count == 1
   112	                && instances.Values.Single() is { Valid: true } and var inst)
   113	            {
   114	                return inst;
   115	            }
   116	
   117	            // Return the autostart, if we can find it.
   118	            // We check both null and "" as we can't write NULL to the config, so we write an empty string instead
   119	            // This is necessary so we can indicate that the user wants to reset the current AutoStartInstance without clearing the config!
   120	            if (Configuration.AutoStartInstance is { Length: > 0 } instName
   121	                && instances.TryGetValue(instName, out GameInstance? autoInst)
   122	                && autoInst.Valid)
   123	            {
   124	                return autoInst;
   125	            }
   126	
   127	            // If we know of no instances, try to find one.
   128	            // Otherwise, we know of too many instances!
   129	            // We don't know which one to pick, so we return null.
   130	            return instances.Count == 0 ? FindAndRegisterDefaultInstances() : null;
   131	        }
   132	
   133	        /// <summary>
   134	        /// Find and register default instances by running
   135	        /// game autodetection code. Registers one per known game,
   136	        /// uses first found as default.
   137	        ///
   138	        /// Returns the resulting game instance if found.
   139	        /// </summary>
   140	        public GameInstance? FindAndRegisterDefaultInstances()
   141	        {
   142	            if (instances.Count != 0)
   143	            {
   144	                throw new GameManagerKraken("Attempted to scan for defaults with instances");
   145	            }
   146	            var found = FindDefaultInstances();
   147	            foreach (var inst in found)
   148	            {
   149	                log.DebugFormat("Registering {0} at {1}...",
   150	                                inst.Name, inst.GameDir);
   151	                AddInstance(inst);
   152	            }
   153	            return found.FirstOrDefault();
   154	        }
   155	
   156	        public GameInstance[] FindDefaultInstances()
   157	        {
   158	            var found = KnownGames.knownGames.SelectMany(g =>
   159	                            SteamLibrary.Games
   160	                                        .Select(sg => sg.Name is string name && sg.GameDir is DirectoryInfo dir
   161	                                                          ? new Tuple<string, DirectoryInfo>(name, dir)
   162	                                                          : null)
   163	                                        .Append(g.MacPath() is DirectoryInfo dir
   164	                                                    ? new Tuple<string, DirectoryInfo>(
   165	                                                        string.Format(Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerAuto,
   166	                                                                      g.ShortName),
   167	                                                        dir)
   168	                                                    : null)
   169	                                        .OfType<Tuple<string, DirectoryInfo>>()
   170	                                        .Select(tuple => tuple.Item1 != null && g.GameInFolder(tuple.Item2)
   171	                                                       ? new GameInstance(g, tuple.Item2.FullName,
   172	                                                                          tuple.Item1 ?? g.ShortName, User)
   173	                                                       : null)
   174	                                        .OfType<GameInstance>())
   175	                                  .Where(inst => inst.Valid)
   176	                                  .ToArray();
   177	            foreach (var group in found.GroupBy(inst => inst.Name))
   178	            {
   179	                if (group.Count() > 1)
   180	                {
   181	                    // Make sure the names are unique
   182	                    int index = 0;
   183	                    foreach (var inst in group)
   184	                    {
   185	                        // Find an unused name
   186	                        string name;
   187	                        do
   188	                        {
   189	                            ++index;
   190	                            name = $"{group.Key} ({++index})";
   191	                        }
   192	                        while (found.Any(other => other.Name == name));
   193	                        inst.Name = name;
   194	                    }
   195	                }
   196	            }
   197	            return found;
   198	        }
   199	
   200	        /// <summary>
   201	        /// Adds a game instance to config.
   202	        /// </summary>
   203	        /// <returns>The resulting GameInstance object</returns>
   204	        /// <exception cref="NotGameDirKraken">Thrown if the instance is not a valid game instance.</exception>
   205	        public GameInstance AddInstance(GameInstance instance)
   206	        {
   207	            if (instance.Valid)
   208	            {
   209	                string name = instance.Name;
   210	                instances.Add(name, instance);
   211	                Configuration.SetRegistryToInstances(instances);
   212	            }
   213	            else
   214	            {
   215	                throw new NotGameDirKraken(instance.GameDir);
   216	            }
   217	            return instance;
   218	        }
   219	
   220	        /// <summary>
   221	        /// Adds a game instance to config.
   222	        /// </summary>
   223	        /// <param name="path">The path of the instance</param>
   224	        /// <param name="name">The name of the instance</param>
   225	        /// <param name="user">IUser object for interaction</param>
   226	        /// <returns>The resulting GameInstance object</returns>
   227	        /// <exception cref="NotGameDirKraken">Thrown if the instance is not a valid game instance.</exception>
   228	        public GameInstance? AddInstance(string path, string name, IUser user)
   229	        {
   230	            var game = DetermineGame(new DirectoryInfo(path), user);
   231	            return game == null ? null : AddInstance(new GameInstance(game, path, name, user));
   232	        }
   233	
   234	        /// <summary>
   235	        /// Clones an existing game installation.
   236	        /// </summary>
   237	        /// <param name="existingInstance">The game instance to clone.</param>
   238	        /// <param name="newName">The name for the new instance.</param>
   239	        /// <param name="newPath">The path where the new instance should be located.</param>
   240	        /// <param name="shareStockFolders">True to make junctions or symlinks to stock folders instead of copying</param>
   241	        /// <exception cref="InstanceNameTakenKraken">Thrown if the instance name is already in use.</exception>
   242	        /// <exception cref="NotGameDirKraken">Thrown by AddInstance() if created instance is not valid, e.g. if something went wrong with copying.</exception>
   243	        /// <exception cref="DirectoryNotFoundKraken">Thrown by CopyDirectory() if directory doesn't exist. Should never be thrown here.</exception>
   244	        /// <exception cref="PathErrorKraken">Thrown by CopyDirectory() if the target folder already exists and is not empty.</exception>
   245	        /// <exception cref="IOException">Thrown by CopyDirectory() if something goes wrong during the process.</exception>
   246	        public void CloneInstance(GameInstance existingInstance,
   247	                                  string       newName,
   248	                                  string       newPath,
   249	                                  bool         shareStockFolders = false)
   250	        {
   251	            CloneInstance(existingInstance, newName, newPath,
   252	                          existingInstance.Game.LeaveEmptyInClones,
   253	                          shareStockFolders);
   254	        }
   255	
   256	        /// <summary>
   257	        /// Clones an existing game installation.
   258	        /// </summary>
   259	        /// <param name="existingInstance">The game instance to clone.</param>
   260	        /// <param name="newName">The name for the new instance.</param>
   261	        /// <param name="newPath">The path where the new instance should be located.</param>
   262	        /// <param name="leaveEmpty">Dirs whose contents should not be copied</param>
   263	        /// <param name="shareStockFolders">True to make junctions or symlinks to stock folders instead of copying</param>
   264	        /// <exception cref="InstanceNameTakenKraken">Thrown if the instance name is already in use.</exception>
   265	        /// <exception cref="NotGameDirKraken">Thrown by AddInstance() if created instance is not valid, e.g. if something went wrong with copying.</exception>
   266	        /// <exception cref="DirectoryNotFoundKraken">Thrown by CopyDirectory() if directory doesn't exist. Should never be thrown here.</exception>
   267	        /// <exception cref="PathErrorKraken">Thrown by CopyDirectory() if the target folder already exists and is not empty.</exception>
   268	        /// <exception cref="IOException">Thrown by CopyDirectory() if something goes wrong during the process.</exception>
   269	        public GameInstance CloneInstance(GameInstance existingInstance,
   270	                                          string       newName,
   271	                                          string       newPath,
   272	                                          string[]     leaveEmpty,
   273	                                          bool         shareStockFolders = false)
   274	        {
   275	            if (HasInstance(newName))
   276	            {
   277	                throw new InstanceNameTakenKraken(newName);
   278	            }
   279	            if (!existingInstance.Valid)
   280	            {
   281	                throw new NotGameDirKraken(existingInstance.GameDir, string.Format(
   282	                    Properties.Resources.GameInstanceCloneInvalid, existingInstance.Game.ShortName));
   283	            }
   284	
   285	            CKANPathUtils.CheckFreeSpace(new DirectoryInfo(newPath) switch
   286	                                         {
   287	                                             { Exists: true } di => di,
   288	                                             var di              => di.Parent ?? di.Root,
   289	                                         },
   290	                                         HardLink.GetDeviceIdentifiers(existingInstance.GameDir,
   291	                                                                       newPath)
   292	                                                 .Distinct()
   293	                                                 .Count() > 1
   294	                                             ? existingInstance.TotalSize
   295	                                             : existingInstance.NonHardLinkableSize(leaveEmpty),
   296	                                         Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerCloneNotEnoughFreeSpace);
   297	
   298	            log.Debug("Copying directory.");
   299	            Utilities.CopyDirectory(existingInstance.GameDir, newPath,
   300	                                    new string[] { "CKAN/registry.locked", "CKAN/playtime.json", "CKAN/GUIConfig.json" },
   301	                                    shareStockFolders ? existingInstance.Game.StockFolders
   302	                                                      : Array.Empty<string>(),
   303	                                    leaveEmpty,
   304	                                    new string[] { "CKAN" });
   305	
   306	            // Add the new instance to the config
   307	            return AddInstance(new GameInstance(existingInstance.Game, newPath, newName, User));
   308	        }
   309	
   310	        /// <summary>
   311	        /// Create a new fake game instance
   312	        /// </summary>
   313	        /// <param name="game">The game of the new instance.</param>
   314	        /// <param name="newName">The name for the new instance.</param>
   315	        /// <param name="newPath">The location of the new instance.</param>
   316	        /// <param name="version">The version of the new instance. Should have a build number.</param>
   317	        /// <param name="dlcs">The IDlcDetector implementations for the DLCs that should be faked and the requested dlc version as a dictionary.</param>
   318	        /// <exception cref="InstanceNameTakenKraken">Thrown if the instance name is already in use.</exception>
   319	        /// <exception cref="NotGameDirKraken">Thrown by AddInstance() if created instance is not valid, e.g. if a write operation didn't complete for whatever reason.</exception>
   320	        public GameInstance FakeInstance(IGame game, string newName, string newPath, GameVersion version,
   321	                                         Dictionary<IDlcDetector, GameVersion>? dlcs = null)
   322	        {
   323	            var txFileMgr = new TxFileManager();
   324	            using (TransactionScope transaction = CkanTransaction.CreateTransactionScope())
   325	            {
   326	                if (HasInstance(newName))
   327	                {
   328	                    throw new InstanceNameTakenKraken(newName);
   329	                }
   330	
   331	                if (!version.WithoutBuild.InBuildMap(game))
   332	                {
   333	                    throw new BadGameVersionKraken(string.Format(
   334	                        Properties.Resources.GameInstanceFakeBadVersion, game.ShortName, version));
   335	                }
   336	                if (Directory.Exists(newPath) && (Directory.GetFiles(newPath).Length != 0 || Directory.GetDirectories(newPath).Length != 0))
   337	                {
   338	                    throw new BadInstallLocationKraken(Properties.Resources.GameInstanceFakeNotEmpty);
   339	                }
   340	
   341	                log.DebugFormat("Creating folder structure and text files at {0} for {1} version {2}", Path.GetFullPath(newPath), game.ShortName, version.ToString());
   342	
   343	                // Create a game root directory, containing a GameData folder, a buildID.txt/buildID64.txt and a readme.txt
   344	                txFileMgr.CreateDirectory(newPath);
   345	                txFileMgr.CreateDirectory(Path.Combine(newPath, game.PrimaryModDirectoryRelative));
   346	                game.RebuildSubdirectories(newPath);
   347	
   348	                foreach (var anchor in game.InstanceAnchorFiles)
   349	                {
   350	                    txFileMgr.WriteAllText(Path.Combine(newPath, anchor),
   351	                                           version.WithoutBuild.ToString(),
   352	                                           Encoding.UTF8);
   353	                }
   354	
   355	                // Don't write the buildID.txts if we have no build, otherwise it would be -1.
   356	                if (version.IsBuildDefined && game is KerbalSpaceProgram)
   357	                {
   358	                    foreach (var b in KspBuildIdVersionProvider.buildIDfilenames)
   359	                    {
   360	                        txFileMgr.WriteAllText(Path.Combine(newPath, b),
   361	                                               string.Format("build id = {0}", version.Build),
   362	                                               Encoding.UTF8);
   363	                    }
   364	                }
   365	
   366	                // Create the readme.txt WITHOUT build number
   367	                txFileMgr.WriteAllText(Path.Combine(newPath, "readme.txt"),
   368	                                       string.Format("Version {0}",
   369	                                                     version.WithoutBuild.ToString()),
   370	                                       Encoding.UTF8);
   371	
   372	                // Create the needed folder structure and the readme.txt for DLCs that should be simulated.
   373	                if (dlcs != null)
   374	                {
   375	                    foreach ((IDlcDetector dlcDetector, GameVersion dlcVersion) in dlcs)
   376	                    {
   377	                        if (!dlcDetector.AllowedOnBaseVersion(version))
   378	                        {
   379	                            throw new WrongGameVersionKraken(
   380	                                version,
   381	                                string.Format(Properties.Resources.GameInstanceFakeDLCNotAllowed,
   382	                                    game.ShortName,
   383	                                    dlcDetector.ReleaseGameVersion,
   384	                                    dlcDetector.IdentifierBaseName));
   385	                        }
   386	
   387	                        string dlcDir = Path.Combine(newPath, dlcDetector.InstallPath());
   388	                        txFileMgr.CreateDirectory(dlcDir);
   389	                        txFileMgr.WriteAllText(
   390	                            Path.Combine(dlcDir, "readme.txt"),
   391	                            string.Format("Version {0}", dlcVersion),
   392	                            Encoding.UTF8);
   393	                    }
   394	                }
   395	
   396	                // Add the new instance to the config
   397	                GameInstance new_instance = new GameInstance(game, newPath, newName, User);
   398	                AddInstance(new_instance);
   399	                transaction.Complete();
   400	                return new_instance;
   401	            }
   402	        }
   403	
   404	        /// <summary>
   405	        /// Given a string returns a unused valid instance name by postfixing the string
   406	        /// </summary>
   407	        /// <returns> A unused valid instance name.</returns>
   408	        /// <param name="name">The name to use as a base.</param>
   409	        /// <exception cref="Kraken">Could not find a valid name.</exception>
   410	        public string GetNextValidInstanceName(string name)
   411	        {
   412	            // Check if the current name is valid
   413	            if (InstanceNameIsValid(name))
   414	            {
   415	                return name;
   416	            }
   417	
   418	            // Try appending a number to the name
   419	            var validName = Enumerable.Repeat(name, 1000)
   420	                .Select((s, i) => s + " (" + i + ")")
   421	                .FirstOrDefault(InstanceNameIsValid);
   422	            if (validName != null)
   423	            {
   424	                return validName;
   425	            }
   426	
   427	            // Check if a name with the current timestamp is valid
   428	            validName = name + " (" + DateTime.Now + ")";
   429	
   430	            if (InstanceNameIsValid(validName))
   431	            {
   432	                return validName;
   433	            }
   434	
   435	            // Give up
   436	            throw new Kraken(Properties.Resources.GameInstanceNoValidName);
   437	        }
   438	
   439	        /// <summary>
   440	        /// Check if the instance name is valid.
   441	        /// </summary>
   442	        /// <returns><c>true</c>, if name is valid, <c>false</c> otherwise.</returns>
   443	        /// <param name="name">Name to check.</param>
   444	        private bool InstanceNameIsValid(string name)
   445	        {
   446	            // Discard null, empty strings and white space only strings.
   447	            // Look for the current name in the list of loaded instances.
   448	            return !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(name) && !HasInstance(name);
   449	        }
   450	
   451	        /// <summary>
   452	        /// Removes the instance from the config and saves.
   453	        /// </summary>
   454	        public void RemoveInstance(string name)
   455	        {
   456	            instances.Remove(name);
   457	            Configuration.SetRegistryToInstances(instances);
   458	        }
   459	
   460	        /// <summary>
   461	        /// Renames an instance in the config and saves.
   462	        /// </summary>
   463	        public void RenameInstance(string from, string to)
   464	        {
   465	            if (from != to)
   466	            {
   467	                if (instances.ContainsKey(to))
   468	                {
   469	                    throw new InstanceNameTakenKraken(to);
   470	                }
   471	                var inst = instances[from];
   472	                instances.Remove(from);
   473	                inst.Name = to;
   474	                instances.Add(to, inst);
   475	                Configuration.SetRegistryToInstances(instances);
   476	            }
   477	        }
   478	
   479	        /// <summary>
   480	        /// Sets the current instance.
   481	        /// Throws an InvalidGameInstanceKraken if not found.
   482	        /// </summary>
   483	        public void SetCurrentInstance(string name)
   484	        {
   485	            if (!instances.TryGetValue(name, out GameInstance? inst))
   486	            {
   487	                throw new InvalidGameInstanceKraken(name);
   488	            }
   489	            else if (!inst.Valid)
   490	            {
   491	                throw new NotGameDirKraken(inst.GameDir);
   492	            }
   493	            else
   494	            {
   495	                SetCurrentInstance(inst);
   496	            }
   497	        }
   498	
   499	        public void SetCurrentInstance(GameInstance? instance)
   500	        {
   501	            var prev = CurrentInstance;
   502	            // Don't try to Dispose a null CurrentInstance.
   503	            if (prev != null && !prev.Equals(instance))
   504	            {
   505	                // Dispose of the old registry manager to release the registry
   506	                // (without accidentally locking/loading/etc it).
   507	                RegistryManager.DisposeInstance(prev);
   508	            }
   509	            CurrentInstance = instance;
   510	            InstanceChanged?.Invoke(prev, instance);
   511	        }
   512	
   513	        public void SetCurrentInstanceByPath(string path)
   514	        {
   515	            if (InstanceAt(path) is GameInstance inst)
   516	            {
   517	                SetCurrentInstance(inst);
   518	            }
   519	        }
   520	
   521	        public GameInstance? InstanceAt(string path)
   522	        {
   523	            var di = new DirectoryInfo(path);
   524	            if (DetermineGame(di, User) is IGame game)
   525	            {
   526	                var inst = new GameInstance(game, path,
   527	                                            Properties.Resources.GameInstanceByPathName,
   528	                                            User);
   529	                if (inst.Valid)
   530	                {
   531	                    return inst;
   532	                }
   533	                else
   534	                {
   535	                    throw new NotGameDirKraken(inst.GameDir);
   536	                }
   537	            }
   538	            return null;
   539	        }
   540	
   541	        /// <summary>
   542	        /// Sets the autostart instance in the config and saves it.
   543	        /// </summary>
   544	        public void SetAutoStart(string name)
   545	        {
   546	            if (!HasInstance(name))
   547	            {
   548	                throw new InvalidGameInstanceKraken(name);
   549	            }
   550	            else if (!instances[name].Valid)
   551	            {
   552	                throw new NotGameDirKraken(instances[name].GameDir);
   553	            }
   554	            Configuration.AutoStartInstance = name;
   555	        }
   556	
   557	        public bool HasInstance(string name)
   558	            => instances.ContainsKey(name);
   559	
   560	        public void ClearAutoStart()
   561	        {
   562	            Configuration.AutoStartInstance = null;
   563	        }
   564	
   565	        private void LoadInstances()
   566	        {
   567	            log.Info("Loading game instances");
   568	
   569	            instances.Clear();
   570	
   571	            foreach (Tuple<string, string, string> instance in Configuration.GetInstances())
   572	            {
   573	                var name = instance.Item1;
   574	                var path = instance.Item2;
   575	                var gameName = instance.Item3;
   576	                try
   577	                {
   578	                    var game = KnownGames.knownGames.FirstOrDefault(g => g.ShortName == gameName)
   579	                        ?? KnownGames.knownGames.First();
   580	                    log.DebugFormat("Loading {0} from {1}", name, path);
   581	                    // Add unconditionally, sort out invalid instances downstream
   582	                    instances.Add(name, new GameInstance(game, path, name, User));
   583	                }
   584	                catch (Exception exc)
   585	                {
   586	                    // Skip malformed instances (e.g. empty path)
   587	                    log.Error($"Failed to load game instance with name=\"{name}\" path=\"{path}\" game=\"{gameName}\"",
   588	                        exc);
   589	                }
   590	            }
   591	        }
   592	
   593	        private void LoadCacheSettings()
   594	        {
   595	            if (Configuration.DownloadCacheDir != null
   596	                && !Directory.Exists(Configuration.DownloadCacheDir))
   597	            {
   598	                try
   599	                {
   600	                    Directory.CreateDirectory(Configuration.DownloadCacheDir);
   601	                }
   602	                catch
   603	                {
   604	                    // Can't create the configured directory, try reverting it to the default
   605	                    Configuration.DownloadCacheDir = null;
   606	                    Directory.CreateDirectory(DefaultDownloadCacheDir);
   607	                }
   608	            }
   609	
   610	            var progress = new ProgressImmediate<int>(p => {});
   611	            if (!TrySetupCache(Configuration.DownloadCacheDir,
   612	                               progress,
   613	                               out string? failReason)
   614	                && Configuration.DownloadCacheDir is { Length: > 0 })
   615	            {
   616	                log.ErrorFormat("Cache not found at configured path {0}: {1}",
   617	                                Configuration.DownloadCacheDir, failReason ?? "");
   618	                // Fall back to default path to minimize chance of ending up in an invalid state at startup
   619	                TrySetupCache(null, progress, out _);
   620	            }
   621	        }
   622	
   623	        /// <summary>
   624	        /// Switch to using a download cache in a new location
   625	        /// </summary>
   626	        /// <param name="path">Location of folder for new cache</param>
   627	        /// <param name="progress">Progress object to report progress to</param>
   628	        /// <param name="failureReason">Contains a human readable failure message if the setup failed</param>
   629	        /// <returns>
   630	        /// true if successful, false otherwise
   631	        /// </returns>
   632	        public bool TrySetupCache(string?        path,
   633	                                  IProgress<int> progress,
   634	                                  [NotNullWhen(false)]
   635	                                  out string?    failureReason)
   636	        {
   637	            var origPath  = Configuration.DownloadCacheDir;
   638	            var origCache = Cache;
   639	            try
   640	            {
   641	                if (path is { Length: > 0 })
   642	                {
   643	                    Cache = new NetModuleCache(this, path);
   644	                    if (path != origPath)
   645	                    {
   646	                        Configuration.DownloadCacheDir = path;
   647	                    }
   648	                }
   649	                else
   650	                {
   651	                    Directory.CreateDirectory(DefaultDownloadCacheDir);
   652	                    Cache = new NetModuleCache(this, DefaultDownloadCacheDir);
   653	                    Configuration.DownloadCacheDir = null;
   654	                }
   655	                if (origPath != null && origCache != null && path != origPath)
   656	                {
   657	                    origCache.GetSizeInfo(out _, out long oldNumBytes, out _);
   658	                    Cache.GetSizeInfo(out _, out _, out long? bytesFree);
   659	
   660	                    if (oldNumBytes > 0)
   661	                    {
   662	                        switch (User.RaiseSelectionDialog(
   663	                                    bytesFree.HasValue
   664	                                        ? string.Format(Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerCacheMigrationPrompt,
   665	                                                        CkanModule.FmtSize(oldNumBytes),
   666	                                                        CkanModule.FmtSize(bytesFree.Value))
   667	                                        : string.Format(Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerCacheMigrationPromptFreeSpaceUnknown,
   668	                                                        CkanModule.FmtSize(oldNumBytes)),
   669	                                    oldNumBytes < (bytesFree ?? 0) ? 0 : 2,
   670	                                    Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerCacheMigrationMove,
   671	                                    Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerCacheMigrationDelete,
   672	                                    Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerCacheMigrationOpen,
   673	                                    Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerCacheMigrationNothing,
   674	                                    Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerCacheMigrationRevert))
   675	                        {
   676	                            case 0:
   677	                                if (oldNumBytes < bytesFree)
   678	                                {
   679	                                    Cache.MoveFrom(new DirectoryInfo(origPath), progress);
   680	                                    CacheChanged?.Invoke(origCache);
   681	                                    origCache.Dispose();
   682	                                }
   683	                                else
   684	                                {
   685	                                    User.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerCacheMigrationNotEnoughFreeSpace);
   686	                                    // Abort since the user picked an option that doesn't work
   687	                                    Cache = origCache;
   688	                                    Configuration.DownloadCacheDir = origPath;
   689	                                    failureReason = "";
   690	                                }
   691	                                break;
   692	
   693	                            case 1:
   694	                                origCache.RemoveAll();
   695	                                CacheChanged?.Invoke(origCache);
   696	                                origCache.Dispose();
   697	                                break;
   698	
   699	                            case 2:
   700	                                Utilities.OpenFileBrowser(origPath);
   701	                                Utilities.OpenFileBrowser(Configuration.DownloadCacheDir ?? DefaultDownloadCacheDir);
   702	                                CacheChanged?.Invoke(origCache);
   703	                                origCache.Dispose();
   704	                                break;
   705	
   706	                            case 3:
   707	                                CacheChanged?.Invoke(origCache);
   708	                                origCache.Dispose();
   709	                                break;
   710	
   711	                            case -1:
   712	                            case 4:
   713	                                Cache = origCache;
   714	                                Configuration.DownloadCacheDir = origPath;
   715	                                failureReason = "";
   716	                                return false;
   717	                        }
   718	                    }
   719	                    else
   720	                    {
   721	                        CacheChanged?.Invoke(origCache);
   722	                        origCache.Dispose();
   723	                    }
   724	                }
   725	                failureReason = null;
   726	                return true;
   727	            }
   728	            catch (DirectoryNotFoundKraken)
   729	            {
   730	                Cache = origCache;
   731	                Configuration.DownloadCacheDir = origPath;
   732	                failureReason = string.Format(Properties.Resources.GameInstancePathNotFound, path);
   733	                return false;
   734	            }
   735	            catch (Exception ex)
   736	            {
   737	                Cache = origCache;
   738	                Configuration.DownloadCacheDir = origPath;
   739	                failureReason = ex.Message;
   740	                return false;
   741	            }
   742	        }
   743	
   744	        /// <summary>
   745	        /// Releases all resource used by the <see cref="GameInstance"/> object.
   746	        /// </summary>
   747	        /// <remarks>Call <see cref="Dispose"/> when you are finished using the <see cref="GameInstance"/>. The <see cref="Dispose"/>
   748	        /// method leaves the <see cref="GameInstance"/> in an unusable state. After calling <see cref="Dispose"/>, you must
   749	        /// release all references to the <see cref="GameInstance"/> so the garbage collector can reclaim the memory that
   750	        /// the <see cref="GameInstance"/> was occupying.</remarks>
   751	        public void Dispose()
   752	        {
   753	            Cache?.Dispose();
   754	            Cache = null;
   755	
   756	            // Attempting to dispose of the related RegistryManager object here is a bad idea, it cause loads of failures
   757	            GC.SuppressFinalize(this);
   758	        }
   759	
   760	        public static bool IsGameInstanceDir(DirectoryInfo path)
   761	            => KnownGames.knownGames.Any(g => g.GameInFolder(path));
   762	
   763	        /// <summary>
   764	        /// Tries to determine the game that is installed at the given path
   765	        /// </summary>
   766	        /// <param name="path">A DirectoryInfo of the path to check</param>
   767	        /// <param name="user">IUser object for interaction</param>
   768	        /// <returns>An instance of the matching game or null if the user cancelled</returns>
   769	        /// <exception cref="NotGameDirKraken">Thrown when no games found</exception>
   770	        public IGame? DetermineGame(DirectoryInfo path, IUser user)
   771	            => KnownGames.knownGames.Where(g => g.GameInFolder(path))
   772	                                    .ToArray()
   773	               switch
   774	               {
   775	                   { Length: 0 }       => throw new NotGameDirKraken(path.FullName),
   776	                   { Length: 1 } games => games.Single(),
   777	                   var games => user.RaiseSelectionDialog(
   778	                                    string.Format(Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerSelectGamePrompt,
   779	                                                  Platform.FormatPath(path.FullName)),
   780	                                    games.Select(g => g.ShortName)
   781	                                         .ToArray())
   782	                                is int selection and >= 0
   783	                                    ? games[selection]
   784	                                    : null
   785	               };
   786	
   787	        public static readonly string DefaultDownloadCacheDir =
   788	            Path.Combine(CKANPathUtils.AppDataPath, "downloads");
   789	    }
   790	}

    35	        /// <summary>
    36	        /// Call a function and take a default action if it throws an exception
    37	        /// </summary>
    38	        /// <typeparam name="T">Return type of the function</typeparam>
    39	        /// <param name="func">Function to call</param>
    40	        /// <param name="onThrow">Function to call if an exception is thrown</param>
    41	        /// <returns>Return value of the function</returns>
    42	        public static T? DefaultIfThrows<T>(Func<T?>             func,
    43	                                            Func<Exception, T?>? onThrow = null) where T : class
    44	        {
    45	            try
    46	            {
    47	                return func();
    48	            }
    49	            catch (Exception exc)
    50	            {
    51	                return onThrow?.Invoke(exc) ?? default;
    52	            }
    53	        }
    54	
    55	        /// <summary>
    56	        /// Extract and rethrow the (first) inner exception if an aggregate exception is thrown
    57	        /// </summary>
    58	        /// <param name="func">Function to call</param>
    59	        /// <returns>Return value of func, unless an exception is thrown</returns>
    60	        public static T WithRethrowInner<T>(Func<T> func)
    61	        {
    62	            try
    63	            {
    64	                return func();
    65	            }
    66	            catch (AggregateException agExc)
    67	            {
    68	                agExc.RethrowInner();
    69	                throw;
    70	            }
    71	        }
    72	
    73	        /// <summary>
    74	        /// Copies a directory and its subdirectories as a transaction
    75	        /// </summary>
    76	        /// <param name="sourceDirPath">Source directory path</param>
    77	        /// <param name="destDirPath">Destination directory path</param>
    78	        /// <param name="fileRelPathsToIgnore">Files to skip</param>
    79	        /// <param name="subFolderRelPathsToSymlink">Relative subdirs that should be symlinked to the originals instead of copied</param>
    80	        /// <param name="subFolderRelPathsToLeaveEmpty">Relative subdirs that should be left empty</param>
    81	        /// <param name="subFolderRelPathsToForbidHardlinks">Relative subdirs that should always have their files copied instead of hardlinked</param>
    82	        public static void CopyDirectory(string   sourceDirPath,
    83	                                         string   destDirPath,
    84	                                         string[] fileRelPathsToIgnore,
    85	                                         string[] subFolderRelPathsToSymlink,
    86	                                         string[] subFolderRelPathsToLeaveEmpty,
    87	                                         string[] subFolderRelPathsToForbidHardlinks)
    88	        {
    89	            using (var transaction = CkanTransaction.CreateTransactionScope())
    90	            {
    91	                CopyDirectory(sourceDirPath, destDirPath, new TxFileManager(),
    92	                              fileRelPathsToIgnore,
    93	                              subFolderRelPathsToSymlink,
    94	                              subFolderRelPathsToLeaveEmpty,
    95	                              subFolderRelPathsToForbidHardlinks);
    96	                transaction.Complete();
    97	            }
    98	        }
    99	
   100	        private static void CopyDirectory(string        sourceDirPath,
   101	                                          string        destDirPath,
   102	                                          TxFileManager txFileMgr,
   103	                                          string[]      fileRelPathsToIgnore,
   104	                                          string[]      subFolderRelPathsToSymlink,
   105	                                          string[]      subFolderRelPathsToLeaveEmpty,
   106	                                          string[]      subFolderRelPathsToForbidHardlinks,
   107	                                          bool          allowHardLinks = true)
   108	        {
   109	            var sourceDir = new DirectoryInfo(sourceDirPath);
   110	            if (!sourceDir.Exists)
   111	            {
   112	                throw new DirectoryNotFoundKraken(
   113	                    sourceDirPath,
   114	                    $"Source directory {sourceDirPath} does not exist or could not be found.");
   115	            }
   116	
   117	            // If the destination directory doesn't exist, create it
   118	            if (!Directory.Exists(destDirPath))
   119	            {
   120	                txFileMgr.CreateDirectory(destDirPath);
   121	            }
   122	            else if (Directory.GetDirectories(destDirPath).Length != 0 || Directory.GetFiles(destDirPath).Length != 0)
   123	            {
   124	                throw new PathErrorKraken(destDirPath,
   125	                                          string.Format(Properties.Resources.DirectoryNotEmpty,
   126	                                                        destDirPath));
   127	            }
   128	
   129	            // Get the files in the directory and copy them to the new location
   130	            foreach (var file in sourceDir.GetFiles())
   131	            {
   132	                if (fileRelPathsToIgnore.Contains(file.Name, Platform.PathComparer))
   133	                {
   134	                    continue;
   135	                }
   136	                if (allowHardLinks)
   137	                {
   138	                    InstalledFilesDeduplicator.CreateOrCopy(file,
   139	                                                            Path.Combine(destDirPath, file.Name),
   140	                                                            txFileMgr);
   141	                }
   142	                else
   143	                {
   144	                    txFileMgr.Copy(file.FullName, Path.Combine(destDirPath, file.Name), false);
   145	                }
   146	            }
   147	
   148	            // Create all first level subdirectories
   149	            foreach (var subdir in sourceDir.GetDirectories())
   150	            {
   151	                var temppath = Path.Combine(destDirPath, subdir.Name);
   152	                // If already a sym link, replicate it in the new location
   153	                if (DirectoryLink.TryGetTarget(subdir.FullName, out string? existingLinkTarget)
   154	                    && existingLinkTarget is not null)
   155	                {
   156	                    DirectoryLink.Create(existingLinkTarget, temppath, txFileMgr);
   157	                }
   158	                else
   159	                {
   160	                    if (subFolderRelPathsToSymlink.Contains(subdir.Name, Platform.PathComparer))
   161	                    {
   162	                        DirectoryLink.Create(subdir.FullName, temppath, txFileMgr);
   163	                    }
   164	                    else
   165	                    {
   166	                        txFileMgr.CreateDirectory(temppath);
   167	
   168	                        if (!subFolderRelPathsToLeaveEmpty.Contains(subdir.Name, Platform.PathComparer))
   169	                        {
   170	                            // Copy subdir contents to new location
   171	                            CopyDirectory(subdir.FullName, temppath, txFileMgr,
   172	                                          SubPaths(subdir.Name, fileRelPathsToIgnore).ToArray(),
   173	                                          SubPaths(subdir.Name, subFolderRelPathsToSymlink).ToArray(),
   174	                                          SubPaths(subdir.Name, subFolderRelPathsToLeaveEmpty).ToArray(),
   175	                                          SubPaths(subdir.Name, subFolderRelPathsToForbidHardlinks).ToArray(),
   176	                                          allowHardLinks && !subFolderRelPathsToForbidHardlinks.Contains(subdir.Name));
   177	                        }
   178	                    }
   179	                }
   180	            }
   181	        }
   182	
   183	        public static long DirectoryNonHardLinkableSize(DirectoryInfo where,
   184	                                                        string[]      fileRelPathsToIgnore,
   185	                                                        string[]      subFolderRelPathsToSymlink,
   186	                                                        string[]      subFolderRelPathsToLeaveEmpty,
   187	                                                        string[]      subFolderRelPathsToForbidHardlinks,
   188	                                                        bool          allowHardLinks = true)
   189	            => where.EnumerateFiles()
   190	                    .Where(f => !fileRelPathsToIgnore.Contains(f.Name, Platform.PathComparer)
   191	                                && !(allowHardLinks && InstalledFilesDeduplicator.UseHardLink(f)))
   192	                    .Sum(f => f.Length)
   193	             + where.EnumerateDirectories()
   194	                    .Where(d => !subFolderRelPathsToLeaveEmpty.Contains(d.Name, Platform.PathComparer)
   195	                                && !subFolderRelPathsToSymlink.Contains(d.Name, Platform.PathComparer))
   196	                    .Sum(d => DirectoryNonHardLinkableSize(
   197	                                  d,
   198	                                  SubPaths(d.Name, fileRelPathsToIgnore).ToArray(),
   199	                                  SubPaths(d.Name, subFolderRelPathsToSymlink).ToArray(),
   200	                                  SubPaths(d.Name, subFolderRelPathsToLeaveEmpty).ToArray(),
   201	                                  SubPaths(d.Name, subFolderRelPathsToForbidHardlinks).ToArray(),
   202	                                  allowHardLinks && !subFolderRelPathsToForbidHardlinks.Contains(d.Name)));
   203	
   204	        // Select only paths within subdir, prune prefixes
   205	        private static IEnumerable<string> SubPaths(string parent, string[] paths)
   206	            => paths.Where(p => p.StartsWith($"{parent}/", Platform.PathComparison))
   207	                    .Select(p => p[(parent.Length + 1)..]);
   208	
   209	        /// <summary>
   210	        /// Launch a URL. For YEARS this was done by Process.Start in a
   211	        /// cross-platform way, but Microsoft chose to break that,
   212	        /// so now every .NET app has to write its own custom code for it,
   213	        /// with special code for each platform.
   214	        /// https://github.com/dotnet/corefx/issues/10361
   215	        /// </summary>
   216	        /// <param name="url">URL to launch</param>
   217	        /// <returns>
   218	        /// true if launched, false otherwise
   219	        /// </returns>
   220	        [ExcludeFromCodeCoverage]
   221	        public static bool ProcessStartURL(string url)
   222	        {
   223	            try
   224	            {
   225	                if (Platform.IsMac)
   226	                {
   227	                    Process.Start("open", $"\"{url}\"");
   228	                    return true;
   229	                }
   230	                else if (Platform.IsUnix)
   231	                {
   232	                    Process.Start("xdg-open", $"\"{url}\"");
   233	                    return true;
   234	                }
   235	                else
   236	                {
   237	                    // Try the old way
   238	                    Process.Start(new ProcessStartInfo(url)
   239	                    {
   240	                        UseShellExecute = true,
   241	                        Verb            = "open"
   242	                    });
   243	                    return true;
   244	                }
   245	            }
   246	            catch (Exception exc)
   247	            {
   248	                log.Error($"Exception for URL {url}", exc);
   249	            }
   250	            return false;
   251	        }
   252	
   253	        [ExcludeFromCodeCoverage]
   254	        public static void OpenFileBrowser(string location)
   255	        {
   256	            // We need the folder of the file
   257	            // Otherwise the OS would try to open the file in its default application
   258	            if (DirPath(location) is string path)
   259	            {
   260	                ProcessStartURL(path);
   261	            }
   262	        }
   263	
   264	        private static string? DirPath(string path)
   265	            => Directory.Exists(path) ? path
   266	             : File.Exists(path) && Path.GetDirectoryName(path) is string parent
   267	                                 && Directory.Exists(parent)
   268	                 ? parent
   269	             : null;
   270	
   271	        private static readonly ILog log = LogManager.GetLogger(typeof(Utilities));
   272	    }
   273	}

2026-05-29 12:32:06,835 - INFO - swea-agent-KSP-CKAN__CKAN-4556 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I understand the issue. The `CopyDirectory` method recursively copies a source directory to a destination directory. The problem is that if the destination directory is a subdirectory of the source directory, it will create an infinite copy loop: the destination directory gets created inside the source, and then when we iterate through subdirectories of the source, we encounter the destination and copy it again, creating a nested copy, ad infinitum (or until disk space runs out).

The fix should be in `CloneInstance` or `CopyDirectory`. The PR description suggests either:
1. Detect when not to copy recursively
2. Use a standard OS copy tool that doesn't do this
3. Throw an error if the canonicalized path of the target folder is a subdirectory of the canonicalized path of the source directory

Let me check if there are any existing tests for this

Now I understand the full picture. The issue is in `Utilities.CopyDirectory`. When the destination path is a subdirectory of the source path, the recursive copy will keep copying the destination folder into itself, creating an infinite loop.

The best approach, as suggested in the PR description, is to check if the destination directory (canonicalized) is a subdirectory of the source directory (canonicalized) and throw an error before starting the copy. Alternatively, we could skip the destination directory during the copy.

Let me check how to get the full/canonical path in .NET:

The fix should be in `CloneInstance` method in `GameInstanceManager.cs` (or in the `CopyDirectory` method in `Utilities.cs`). Let's think about the best place:

1. The fix could be in `CloneInstance` - check if the new path is a subdirectory of the source path before copying
2. The fix could be in `CopyDirectory` - check generically

Since `CopyDirectory` is a general-purpose utility and the bug report is specifically about cloning, the fix should probably go in `CloneInstance`. But it could also be argued that `CopyDirectory` should handle this case. Let me put the check in `CloneInstance` since that's the specific use case and it's better to catch this early with a clear error message.

Let me also check the `CKANPathUtils` class for any relevant path

     1	using System;
     2	using System.IO;
     3	
     4	using log4net;
     5	
     6	using CKAN.Extensions;
     7	
     8	namespace CKAN.IO
     9	{
    10	    public static class CKANPathUtils
    11	    {
    12	        /// <summary>
    13	        /// Path to save CKAN data shared across all game instances
    14	        /// </summary>
    15	        public static readonly string AppDataPath = Path.Combine(
    16	            Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.LocalApplicationData),
    17	            Meta.ProductName);
    18	
    19	        private static readonly ILog log = LogManager.GetLogger(typeof(CKANPathUtils));
    20	
    21	        /// <summary>
    22	        /// Normalizes the path by replacing all \ with / and removing any trailing slash.
    23	        /// </summary>
    24	        /// <param name="path">The path to normalize</param>
    25	        /// <returns>The normalized path</returns>
    26	        public static string NormalizePath(string path)
    27	            => path.Length < 2 ? path.Replace('\\', '/')
    28	                               : path.Replace('\\', '/').TrimEnd('/');
    29	
    30	        /// <summary>
    31	        /// Converts a path to one relative to the root provided.
    32	        /// Please use KSP.ToRelative when working with gamedirs.
    33	        /// Throws a PathErrorKraken if the path is not absolute, not inside the root,
    34	        /// or either argument is null.
    35	        /// </summary>
    36	        public static string ToRelative(string path, string root)
    37	        {
    38	            // We have to normalise before we check for rootedness,
    39	            // otherwise backslash separators fail on Linux.
    40	
    41	            path = NormalizePath(path);
    42	            root = NormalizePath(root);
    43	
    44	            if (!Path.IsPathRooted(path))
    45	            {
    46	                throw new PathErrorKraken(path, string.Format(
    47	                    Properties.Resources.PathUtilsNotAbsolute, path));
    48	            }
    49	
    50	            if (!path.StartsWith(root, Platform.PathComparison))
    51	            {
    52	                throw new PathErrorKraken(path, string.Format(
    53	                    Properties.Resources.PathUtilsNotInside, path, root));
    54	            }
    55	
    56	            // Strip off the root, then remove any slashes at the beginning
    57	            return path[root.Length..].TrimStart('/');
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        /// <summary>
    61	        /// Returns root/path, but checks that root is absolute,
    62	        /// path is relative, and normalises everything for great justice.
    63	        /// Please use KSP.ToAbsolute if converting from a KSP gamedir.
    64	        /// Throws a PathErrorKraken if anything goes wrong.
    65	        /// </summary>
    66	        public static string ToAbsolute(string path, string root)
    67	        {
    68	            path = NormalizePath(path);
    69	            root = NormalizePath(root);
    70	
    71	            if (Path.IsPathRooted(path))
    72	            {
    73	                throw new PathErrorKraken(
    74	                    path,
    75	                    string.Format(Properties.Resources.PathUtilsAlreadyAbsolute, path)
    76	                );
    77	            }
    78	
    79	            if (!Path.IsPathRooted(root))
    80	            {
    81	                throw new PathErrorKraken(
    82	                    root,
    83	                    string.Format(Properties.Resources.PathUtilsNotRoot, root)
    84	                );
    85	            }
    86	
    87	            // Why normalise it AGAIN? Because Path.Combine can insert
    88	            // the un-prettiest slashes.
    89	            return NormalizePath(Path.Combine(root, path));
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        public static void CheckFreeSpace(DirectoryInfo where,
    93	                                          long          bytesToStore,
    94	                                          string        errorDescription)
    95	        {
    96	            if (bytesToStore > 0
    97	                && where.GetDrive()?.AvailableFreeSpace is long bytesFree)
    98	            {
    99	                if (bytesToStore > bytesFree) {
   100	                    throw new NotEnoughSpaceKraken(errorDescription, where,
   101	                                                   bytesFree, bytesToStore);
   102	                }
   103	                log.DebugFormat("Storing {0} to {1} ({2} free)...",
   104	                                CkanModule.FmtSize(bytesToStore),
   105	                                where.FullName,
   106	                                CkanModule.FmtSize(bytesFree));
   107	            }
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        public static bool PathEquals(this FileSystemInfo a,
   111	                                      FileSystemInfo      b)
   112	            => NormalizePath(a.FullName).Equals(NormalizePath(b.FullName),
   113	                                                Platform.PathComparison);
   114	
   115	    }
   116	}

using System;
using System.IO;
using CKAN;
using CKAN.IO;
using Tests.Data;

class Reproduce {
    static void Main() {
        // Create a source directory
        string sourceDir = Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), "ckan_test_source_" + Guid.NewGuid().ToString("N"));
        Directory.CreateDirectory(sourceDir);
        File.WriteAllText(Path.Combine(sourceDir, "file1.txt"), "test content");
        Directory.CreateDirectory(Path.Combine(sourceDir, "subdir"));
        File.WriteAllText(Path.Combine(sourceDir, "subdir", "file2.txt"), "more content");

        // Target is a subdirectory of source
        string targetDir = Path.Combine(sourceDir, "clone_target");

        Console.WriteLine($"Source: {sourceDir}");
        Console.WriteLine($"Target: {targetDir}");
        Console.WriteLine($"Is target subdirectory of source? {targetDir.StartsWith(sourceDir)}");

        try {
            Utilities.CopyDirectory(sourceDir, targetDir,
                                    Array.Empty<string>(), Array.Empty<string>(),
                                    Array.Empty<string>(), Array.Empty<string>());
            Console.WriteLine("Copy completed (this shouldn't happen without fix)");
            
            // Show what happened
            Console.WriteLine("\nContents after copy:");
            foreach (var f in Directory.GetFiles(targetDir, "*", SearchOption.AllDirectories)) {
                Console.WriteLine($"  {f}");
            }
        } catch (Exception ex) {
            Console.WriteLine($"Exception: {ex.GetType().Name}: {ex.Message}");
        }
        
        // Cleanup
        try { Directory.Delete(sourceDir, true); } catch {}
    }
}
EOF

The fix should be in `CloneInstance` in `GameInstanceManager.cs` to check if the new path is a subdirectory of the existing instance's game directory. If so, it should throw an error.

Let me also think about edge cases:
1. The paths could be the same (target == source)
2. The target could be a subdirectory of the source (the reported bug)
3. The source could be a subdirectory of the target (this is fine for copying, but could also be checked)
4. Symbolic links could make paths appear different but still point to the same location
5. Case-insensitive file systems on Windows/Linux

The best approach is to use `Path.GetFullPath` to get canonical paths, then check if one is a prefix of the other.

Let me now implement the fix

🎬 ACTION
