        }' --new_str 'public GameInstance CloneInstance(GameInstance existingInstance,
                                          string       newName,
                                          string       newPath,
                                          string[]     leaveEmpty,
                                          bool         shareStockFolders = false)
        {
            if (HasInstance(newName))
            {
                throw new InstanceNameTakenKraken(newName);
            }
            if (!existingInstance.Valid)
            {
                throw new NotGameDirKraken(existingInstance.GameDir, string.Format(
                    Properties.Resources.GameInstanceCloneInvalid, existingInstance.Game.ShortName));
            }

            // Make sure we are not cloning to a subdirectory of the source,
            // which would cause an infinite recursive copy
            var fullExistingPath = Path.GetFullPath(existingInstance.GameDir);
            var fullNewPath      = Path.GetFullPath(newPath);
            if (fullNewPath.StartsWith(fullExistingPath + Path.DirectorySeparatorChar,
                                       Platform.PathComparison)
                || fullNewPath.Equals(fullExistingPath, Platform.PathComparison))
            {
                throw new PathErrorKraken(newPath, string.Format(
                    Properties.Resources.GameInstanceCloneTargetSubdirOfSource,
                    fullNewPath, fullExistingPath));
            }

            CKANPathUtils.CheckFreeSpace(new DirectoryInfo(newPath) switch
                                         {
                                             { Exists: true } di => di,
                                             var di              => di.Parent ?? di.Root,
                                         },
                                         HardLink.GetDeviceIdentifiers(existingInstance.GameDir,
                                                                       newPath)
                                                 .Distinct()
                                                 .Count() > 1
                                             ? existingInstance.TotalSize
                                             : existingInstance.NonHardLinkableSize(leaveEmpty),
                                         Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerCloneNotEnoughFreeSpace);

            log.Debug("Copying directory.");
            Utilities.CopyDirectory(existingInstance.GameDir, newPath,
                                    new string[] { "CKAN/registry.locked", "CKAN/playtime.json", "CKAN/GUIConfig.json" },
                                    shareStockFolders ? existingInstance.Game.StockFolders
                                                      : Array.Empty<string>(),
                                    leaveEmpty,
                                    new string[] { "CKAN" });

            // Add the new instance to the config
            return AddInstance(new GameInstance(existingInstance.Game, newPath, newName, User));
        }'

2026-05-29 12:35:34,894 - INFO - swea-agent-KSP-CKAN__CKAN-4556 - 🤖 MODEL INPUT
OBSERVATION:

        public GameInstance CloneInstance(GameInstance existingInstance,
                                          string       newName,
                                          string       newPath,
                                          string[]     leaveEmpty,
                                          bool         shareStockFolders = false)
        {
            if (HasInstance(newName))
            {
                throw new InstanceNameTakenKraken(newName);
            }
            if (!existingInstance.Valid)
            {
                throw new NotGameDirKraken(existingInstance.GameDir, string.Format(
                    Properties.Resources.GameInstanceCloneInvalid, existingInstance.Game.ShortName));
            }

            CKANPathUtils.CheckFreeSpace(new DirectoryInfo(newPath) switch
                                         {
                                             { Exists: true } di => di,
                                             var di              => di.Parent ?? di.Root,
                                         },
                                         HardLink.GetDeviceIdentifiers(existingInstance.GameDir,
                                                                       newPath)
                                                 .Distinct()
                                                 .Count() > 1
                                             ? existingInstance.TotalSize
                                             : existingInstance.NonHardLinkableSize(leaveEmpty),
                                         Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerCloneNotEnoughFreeSpace);

            log.Debug("Copying directory.");
            Utilities.CopyDirectory(existingInstance.GameDir, newPath,
                                    new string[] { "CKAN/registry.locked", "CKAN/playtime.json", "CKAN/GUIConfig.json" },
                                    shareStockFolders ? existingInstance.Game.StockFolders
                                                      : Array.Empty<string>(),
                                    leaveEmpty,
                                    new string[] { "CKAN" });

            // Add the new instance to the config
            return AddInstance(new GameInstance(existingInstance.Game, newPath, newName, User));
        }

        public GameInstance CloneInstance(GameInstance existingInstance,
                                          string       newName,
                                          string       newPath,
                                          string[]     leaveEmpty,
                                          bool         shareStockFolders = false)
        {
            if (HasInstance(newName))
            {
                throw new InstanceNameTakenKraken(newName);
            }
            if (!existingInstance.Valid)
            {
                throw new NotGameDirKraken(existingInstance.GameDir, string.Format(
                    Properties.Resources.GameInstanceCloneInvalid, existingInstance.Game.ShortName));
            }


            // Make sure we are not cloning to a subdirectory of the source,
            // which would cause an infinite recursive copy
            var fullExistingPath = Path.GetFullPath(existingInstance.GameDir);
            var fullNewPath      = Path.GetFullPath(newPath);
            if (fullNewPath.StartsWith(fullExistingPath + Path.DirectorySeparatorChar,
                                                 Platform.PathComparison)
                || fullNewPath.Equals(fullExistingPath, Platform.PathComparison))
            {
                throw new PathErrorKraken(newPath, string.Format(
                    Properties.Resources.GameInstanceCloneTargetSubdirOfSource,
                    fullNewPath, fullExistingPath));
            }

            CKANPathUtils.CheckFreeSpace(new DirectoryInfo(newPath) switch
                                         {
                                             { Exists: true } di => di,
                                             var di              => di.Parent ?? di.Root,
                                         },
                                         HardLink.GetDeviceIdentifiers(existingInstance.GameDir,
                                                                       newPath)
                                                 .Distinct()
                                                 .Count() > 1
                                             ? existingInstance.TotalSize
                                             : existingInstance.NonHardLinkableSize(leaveEmpty),
                                         Properties.Resources.GameInstanceManagerCloneNotEnoughFreeSpace);

            log.Debug("Copying directory.");
            Utilities.CopyDirectory(existingInstance.GameDir, newPath,
                                    new string[] { "CKAN/registry.locked", "CKAN/playtime.json", "CKAN/GUIConfig.json" },
                                    shareStockFolders ? existingInstance.Game.StockFolders
                                                      : Array.Empty<string>(),
                                    leaveEmpty,
                                    new string[] { "CKAN" });

            // Add the new instance to the config

    16	    [ExcludeFromCodeCoverage]
    17	    internal class InstanceSubOptions : VerbCommandOptions
    18	    {
    19	        [VerbOption("list",    HelpText = "List game instances")]
    20	        public ListInstancesOptions? ListOptions { get; set; }
    21	
    22	        [VerbOption("add",     HelpText = "Add a game instance")]
    23	        public AddOptions?     AddOptions     { get; set; }
    24	
    25	        [VerbOption("clone",   HelpText = "Clone an existing game instance")]
    26	        public CloneOptions?   CloneOptions   { get; set; }
    27	
    28	        [VerbOption("rename",  HelpText = "Rename a game instance")]
    29	        public RenameOptions?  RenameOptions  { get; set; }
    30	
    31	        [VerbOption("forget",  HelpText = "Forget a game instance")]
    32	        public ForgetOptions?  ForgetOptions  { get; set; }
    33	
    34	        [VerbOption("default", HelpText = "Set the default game instance")]
    35	        public DefaultOptions? DefaultOptions { get; set; }
    36	
    37	        [VerbOption("fake",    HelpText = "Fake a game instance")]
    38	        public FakeOptions?    FakeOptions    { get; set; }
    39	
    40	        [HelpVerbOption]
    41	        public string GetUsage(string verb)
    42	        {
    43	            var ht = HelpText.AutoBuild(this, verb);
    44	            foreach (var h in GetHelp(verb))
    45	            {
    46	                ht.AddPreOptionsLine(h);
    47	            }
    48	            return ht;
    49	        }
    50	
    51	        [ExcludeFromCodeCoverage]
    52	        public static IEnumerable<string> GetHelp(string verb)
    53	        {
    54	            // Add a usage prefix line
    55	            yield return " ";
    56	            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(verb))
    57	            {
    58	                yield return $"ckan instance - {Properties.Resources.InstanceHelpSummary}";
    59	                yield return $"{Properties.Resources.Usage}: ckan instance <{Properties.Resources.Command}> [{Properties.Resources.Options}]";
    60	            }
    61	            else
    62	            {
    63	                yield return "instance " + verb + " - " + GetDescription(typeof(InstanceSubOptions), verb);
    64	                switch (verb)
    65	                {
    66	                    // First the commands with three string arguments
    67	                    case "fake":
    68	                        yield return $"{Properties.Resources.Usage}: ckan instance {verb} [{Properties.Resources.Options}] name path version [--game KSP|KSP2] [--MakingHistory <version>] [--BreakingGround <version>]";
    69	                        break;
    70	
    71	                    case "clone":
    72	                        yield return $"{Properties.Resources.Usage}: ckan instance {verb} [{Properties.Resources.Options}] instanceNameOrPath newname newpath";
    73	                        break;
    74	
    75	                    // Second the commands with two string arguments
    76	                    case "add":
    77	                        yield return $"{Properties.Resources.Usage}: ckan instance {verb} [{Properties.Resources.Options}] name url";
    78	                        break;
    79	                    case "rename":
    80	                        yield return $"{Properties.Resources.Usage}: ckan instance {verb} [{Properties.Resources.Options}] oldname newname";
    81	                        break;
    82	
    83	                    // Now the commands with one string argument
    84	                    case "remove":
    85	                    case "forget":
    86	                    case "use":
    87	                    case "default":
    88	                        yield return $"{Properties.Resources.Usage}: ckan instance {verb} [{Properties.Resources.Options}] name";
    89	                        break;
    90	
    91	                    // Now the commands with only --flag type options
    92	                    case "list":
    93	                    default:
    94	                        yield return $"{Properties.Resources.Usage}: ckan instance {verb} [{Properties.Resources.Options}]";
    95	                        break;
    96	
    97	                }
    98	            }
    99	        }
   100	    }

   157	    public class GameInstance : ISubCommand
   158	    {
   159	        public GameInstance(GameInstanceManager manager,
   160	                            IUser               user)
   161	        {
   162	            Manager = manager;
   163	            this.user = user;
   164	        }
   165	
   166	        // This is required by ISubCommand
   167	        public int RunSubCommand(CommonOptions?    opts,
   168	                                 SubCommandOptions unparsed)
   169	        {
   170	            string[] args = unparsed.options.ToArray();
   171	
   172	            #region Aliases
   173	
   174	            for (int i = 0; i < args.Length; i++)
   175	            {
   176	                switch (args[i])
   177	                {
   178	                    case "use":
   179	                        args[i] = "default";
   180	                        break;
   181	
   182	                    default:
   183	                        break;
   184	                }
   185	            }
   186	
   187	            #endregion
   188	
   189	            int exitCode = Exit.OK;
   190	            // Parse and process our sub-verbs
   191	            Parser.Default.ParseArgumentsStrict(args, new InstanceSubOptions(), (option, suboptions) =>
   192	            {
   193	                // ParseArgumentsStrict calls us unconditionally, even with bad arguments
   194	                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(option) && suboptions != null)
   195	                {
   196	                    CommonOptions options = (CommonOptions)suboptions;
   197	                    options.Merge(opts);
   198	                    exitCode = options.Handle(Manager, user);
   199	                    if (exitCode == Exit.OK)
   200	                    {
   201	                        exitCode = suboptions switch
   202	                        {
   203	                            ListInstancesOptions => ListInstances(),
   204	                            AddOptions     opts  => AddInstance(opts),
   205	                            CloneOptions   opts  => CloneInstance(opts),
   206	                            RenameOptions  opts  => RenameInstance(opts),
   207	                            ForgetOptions  opts  => ForgetInstance(opts),
   208	                            DefaultOptions opts  => SetDefaultInstance(opts),
   209	                            FakeOptions    opts  => FakeNewGameInstance(opts),
   210	                            // The parser makes this case impossible,
   211	                            // but the compiler doesn't know that
   212	                            _                    => UnknownCommand(option),
   213	                        };
   214	                    }
   215	                }
   216	            }, () => { exitCode = MainClass.AfterHelp(user); });
   217	            return exitCode;
   218	        }
   219	
   220	        private readonly IUser               user;
   221	        private readonly GameInstanceManager Manager;
   222	
   223	        #region option functions
   224	
   225	        private int ListInstances()
   226	        {
   227	            var output = Manager.Instances.Values
   228	                .OrderByDescending(i => i.Name == Manager.Configuration.AutoStartInstance)
   229	                .ThenByDescending(i => i.Game.FirstReleaseDate)
   230	                .ThenByDescending(i => i.Version() ?? GameVersion.Any)
   231	                .ThenBy(i => i.Name)
   232	                .Select(i => new Tuple<string, string, string, string, string>(
   233	                                i.Name,
   234	                                i.Game.ShortName,
   235	                                i.Version()?.ToString() ?? Properties.Resources.InstanceListNoVersion,
   236	                                i.Name == Manager.Configuration.AutoStartInstance
   237	                                    ? Properties.Resources.InstanceListYes
   238	                                    : Properties.Resources.InstanceListNo,
   239	                                Platform.FormatPath(i.GameDir)))
   240	                .ToList();
   241	
   242	            if (output != null && user != null)
   243	            {
   244	                var nameHeader    = Properties.Resources.InstanceListNameHeader;
   245	                var gameHeader    = Properties.Resources.InstanceListGameHeader;
   246	                var versionHeader = Properties.Resources.InstanceListVersionHeader;
   247	                var defaultHeader = Properties.Resources.InstanceListDefaultHeader;
   248	                var pathHeader    = Properties.Resources.InstanceListPathHeader;
   249	
   250	                var nameWidth    = output.Select(i => i.Item1).Append(nameHeader).Max(i => i.Length);
   251	                var gameWidth    = output.Select(i => i.Item2).Append(gameHeader).Max(i => i.Length);
   252	                var versionWidth = output.Select(i => i.Item3).Append(versionHeader).Max(i => i.Length);
   253	                var defaultWidth = output.Select(i => i.Item4).Append(defaultHeader).Max(i => i.Length);
   254	                var pathWidth    = output.Select(i => i.Item5).Append(pathHeader).Max(i => i.Length);
   255	
   256	                var columnFormat = string.Join("  ", $"{{0,-{nameWidth}}}",
   257	                                                     $"{{1,-{gameWidth}}}",
   258	                                                     $"{{2,-{versionWidth}}}",
   259	                                                     $"{{3,-{defaultWidth}}}",
   260	                                                     $"{{4,-{pathWidth}}}");
   261	
   262	                user.RaiseMessage(columnFormat,
   263	                                  nameHeader, gameHeader, versionHeader, defaultHeader, pathHeader);
   264	
   265	                user.RaiseMessage(columnFormat, new string('-', nameWidth),
   266	                                                new string('-', gameWidth),
   267	                                                new string('-', versionWidth),
   268	                                                new string('-', defaultWidth),
   269	                                                new string('-', pathWidth));
   270	
   271	                foreach (var line in output)
   272	                {
   273	                    user.RaiseMessage(columnFormat, line.Item1, line.Item2, line.Item3, line.Item4, line.Item5);
   274	                }
   275	
   276	                return Exit.OK;
   277	            }
   278	            return Exit.ERROR;
   279	        }
   280	
   281	        private int AddInstance(AddOptions options)
   282	        {
   283	            if (options.name == null || options.path == null)
   284	            {
   285	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.ArgumentMissing);
   286	                PrintUsage("add");
   287	                return Exit.BADOPT;
   288	            }
   289	
   290	            if (Manager.HasInstance(options.name))
   291	            {
   292	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceAddDuplicate, options.name);
   293	                return Exit.BADOPT;
   294	            }
   295	
   296	            try
   297	            {
   298	                if (user != null)
   299	                {
   300	                    string path = options.path;
   301	                    Manager.AddInstance(path, options.name, user);
   302	                    user.RaiseMessage(Properties.Resources.InstanceAdded, options.name, options.path);
   303	                }
   304	                return Exit.OK;
   305	            }
   306	            catch (NotGameDirKraken ex)
   307	            {
   308	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceNotInstance, ex.path);
   309	                return Exit.BADOPT;
   310	            }
   311	        }
   312	
   313	        private int CloneInstance(CloneOptions options)
   314	        {
   315	            if (options.nameOrPath == null || options.new_name == null || options.new_path == null)
   316	            {
   317	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.ArgumentMissing);
   318	                PrintUsage("clone");
   319	                return Exit.BADOPT;
   320	            }
   321	
   322	            // Parse all options
   323	            string instanceNameOrPath = options.nameOrPath;
   324	            string newName = options.new_name;
   325	            string newPath = options.new_path;
   326	
   327	            log.Info("Cloning the game instance: " + options.nameOrPath);
   328	
   329	            try
   330	            {
   331	                // Try instanceNameOrPath as name and search the registry for it.
   332	                if (Manager.HasInstance(instanceNameOrPath))
   333	                {
   334	                    CKAN.GameInstance[] listOfInstances = Manager.Instances.Values.ToArray();
   335	                    foreach (CKAN.GameInstance instance in listOfInstances)
   336	                    {
   337	                        if (instance.Name == instanceNameOrPath)
   338	                        {
   339	                            // Found it, now clone it.
   340	                            Manager.CloneInstance(instance, newName, newPath, options.shareStock);
   341	                            break;
   342	                        }
   343	                    }
   344	                }
   345	                // Try to use instanceNameOrPath as a path and create a new game instance.
   346	                // If it's valid, go on.
   347	                else if (Manager.InstanceAt(instanceNameOrPath) is CKAN.GameInstance instance && instance.Valid)
   348	                {
   349	                    Manager.CloneInstance(instance, newName, newPath, options.shareStock);
   350	                }
   351	                // There is no instance with this name or at this path.
   352	                else
   353	                {
   354	                    user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceCloneNotFound, instanceNameOrPath);
   355	                    ListInstances();
   356	                    return Exit.ERROR;
   357	                }
   358	            }
   359	            catch (Kraken k)
   360	            {
   361	                user.RaiseError("{0}", k.Message);
   362	                return Exit.ERROR;
   363	            }
   364	            catch (Exception e)
   365	            {
   366	                // Something went wrong copying the files. Contains a message.
   367	                log.Error(e);
   368	                return Exit.ERROR;
   369	            }
   370	
   371	            // Test if the instance was added to the registry.
   372	            // No need to test if valid, because this is done in AddInstance(),
   373	            // so if something went wrong, HasInstance is false.
   374	            if (Manager.HasInstance(newName))
   375	            {
   376	                return Exit.OK;
   377	            }
   378	            else
   379	            {
   380	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceCloneFailed);
   381	                return Exit.ERROR;
   382	            }
   383	        }
   384	
   385	        private int RenameInstance(RenameOptions options)
   386	        {
   387	            if (options.old_name == null || options.new_name == null)
   388	            {
   389	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.ArgumentMissing);
   390	                PrintUsage("rename");
   391	                return Exit.BADOPT;
   392	            }
   393	
   394	            if (!Manager.HasInstance(options.old_name))
   395	            {
   396	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceNotFound, options.old_name);
   397	                return Exit.BADOPT;
   398	            }
   399	
   400	            if (Manager.HasInstance(options.new_name))
   401	            {
   402	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceAddDuplicate, options.old_name);
   403	                return Exit.BADOPT;
   404	            }
   405	
   406	            Manager.RenameInstance(options.old_name, options.new_name);
   407	
   408	            user.RaiseMessage(Properties.Resources.InstanceRenamed, options.old_name, options.new_name);
   409	            return Exit.OK;
   410	        }
   411	
   412	        private int ForgetInstance(ForgetOptions options)
   413	        {
   414	            if (options.name == null)
   415	            {
   416	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.ArgumentMissing);
   417	                PrintUsage("forget");
   418	                return Exit.BADOPT;
   419	            }
   420	
   421	            if (!Manager.HasInstance(options.name))
   422	            {
   423	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceNotFound, options.name);
   424	                return Exit.BADOPT;
   425	            }
   426	
   427	            Manager.RemoveInstance(options.name);
   428	
   429	            user.RaiseMessage(Properties.Resources.InstanceForgot, options.name);
   430	            return Exit.OK;
   431	        }
   432	
   433	        private int SetDefaultInstance(DefaultOptions options)
   434	        {
   435	            var name = options.name;
   436	            // Oh right, this is that one that didn't work AT ALL at one point
   437	            if (name == null)
   438	            {
   439	                // No input argument from the user. Present a list of the possible instances.
   440	
   441	                try
   442	                {
   443	                    // If there is a default instance, its index is passed first
   444	                    var defaultInstance = Manager.Configuration.AutoStartInstance;
   445	                    int result = user.RaiseSelectionDialog(
   446	                                     $"default <name> - {Properties.Resources.InstanceDefaultArgumentMissing}",
   447	                                     (defaultInstance == null || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(defaultInstance)
   448	                                         ? Enumerable.Empty<object>()
   449	                                         : Enumerable.Repeat((object)Manager.Instances.IndexOfKey(defaultInstance), 1))
   450	                                         .Concat(Manager.Instances.Select(kvp => string.Format("\"{0}\" - {1}",
   451	                                                                                               kvp.Key, kvp.Value.GameDir)))
   452	                                         .ToArray());
   453	                    if (result < 0)
   454	                    {
   455	                        return Exit.BADOPT;
   456	                    }
   457	                    name = Manager.Instances.ElementAt(result).Key;
   458	                }
   459	                catch (Kraken)
   460	                {
   461	                    return Exit.BADOPT;
   462	                }
   463	            }
   464	
   465	            if (name != null)
   466	            {
   467	                if (!Manager.Instances.ContainsKey(name))
   468	                {
   469	                    user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceNotFound, name);
   470	                    return Exit.BADOPT;
   471	                }
   472	
   473	                try
   474	                {
   475	                    Manager.SetAutoStart(name);
   476	                }
   477	                catch (NotGameDirKraken k)
   478	                {
   479	                    user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceNotInstance, k.path);
   480	                    return Exit.BADOPT;
   481	                }
   482	
   483	                user.RaiseMessage(Properties.Resources.InstanceDefaultSet, name);
   484	                return Exit.OK;
   485	            }
   486	            return Exit.BADOPT;
   487	        }
   488	
   489	        /// <summary>
   490	        /// Creates a new fake game instance after the conditions CKAN tests for valid game directories.
   491	        /// Used for developing and testing purposes.
   492	        /// </summary>
   493	        private int FakeNewGameInstance(FakeOptions options)
   494	        {
   495	            int error()
   496	            {
   497	                log.Debug("Instance faking failed, see console output for details.");
   498	                return Exit.ERROR;
   499	            }
   500	
   501	            int badArgument()
   502	            {
   503	                log.Debug("Instance faking failed: bad argument(s). See console output for details.");
   504	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceFakeBadArguments);
   505	                return Exit.BADOPT;
   506	            }
   507	
   508	
   509	            if (options.name == null || options.path == null || options.version == null)
   510	            {
   511	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.ArgumentMissing);
   512	                PrintUsage("fake");
   513	                return Exit.BADOPT;
   514	            }
   515	
   516	            log.Debug("Parsing arguments...");
   517	            // Parse all options
   518	            string instanceName = options.name;
   519	            string path = options.path;
   520	            GameVersion? version;
   521	            bool setDefault = options.setDefault;
   522	            var game = KnownGames.GameByShortName(options.gameId ?? "");
   523	            if (game == null)
   524	            {
   525	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceFakeBadGame, options.gameId ?? "");
   526	                return badArgument();
   527	            }
   528	
   529	            // options.<DLC>Version is "none" if the DLC should not be simulated.
   530	            var dlcs = new Dictionary<DLC.IDlcDetector, GameVersion>();
   531	            if (options.makingHistoryVersion != null && options.makingHistoryVersion.ToLower() != "none")
   532	            {
   533	                if (GameVersion.TryParse(options.makingHistoryVersion, out GameVersion? ver))
   534	                {
   535	                    dlcs.Add(new MakingHistoryDlcDetector(), ver);
   536	                }
   537	                else
   538	                {
   539	                    user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceFakeMakingHistory);
   540	                    return badArgument();
   541	                }
   542	            }
   543	            if (options.breakingGroundVersion != null && options.breakingGroundVersion.ToLower() != "none")
   544	            {
   545	                if (GameVersion.TryParse(options.breakingGroundVersion, out GameVersion? ver))
   546	                {
   547	                    dlcs.Add(new BreakingGroundDlcDetector(), ver);
   548	                }
   549	                else
   550	                {
   551	                    user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceFakeBreakingGround);
   552	                    return badArgument();
   553	                }
   554	            }
   555	
   556	            // Parse the choosen game version
   557	            try
   558	            {
   559	                version = GameVersion.Parse(options.version);
   560	            }
   561	            catch (FormatException)
   562	            {
   563	                // Thrown if there is anything besides numbers and points in the version string or a different syntactic error.
   564	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceFakeVersion);
   565	                return badArgument();
   566	            }
   567	
   568	            // Get the full version including build number.
   569	            try
   570	            {
   571	                version = version.RaiseVersionSelectionDialog(game, user);
   572	            }
   573	            catch (BadGameVersionKraken)
   574	            {
   575	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceFakeBadGameVersion);
   576	                return badArgument();
   577	            }
   578	            catch (CancelledActionKraken)
   579	            {
   580	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceFakeCancelled);
   581	                return error();
   582	            }
   583	
   584	            if (version == null)
   585	            {
   586	                return error();
   587	            }
   588	
   589	            user.RaiseMessage(Properties.Resources.InstanceFakeCreating,
   590	                              instanceName, path, version.ToString() ?? "");
   591	            log.Debug("Faking instance...");
   592	
   593	            try
   594	            {
   595	                // Pass all arguments to CKAN.GameInstanceManager.FakeInstance() and create a new one.
   596	                Manager.FakeInstance(game, instanceName, path, version, dlcs);
   597	                if (setDefault)
   598	                {
   599	                    user.RaiseMessage(Properties.Resources.InstanceFakeDefault);
   600	                    Manager.SetAutoStart(instanceName);
   601	                }
   602	            }
   603	            catch (InstanceNameTakenKraken kraken)
   604	            {
   605	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceDuplicate, kraken.instName);
   606	                return badArgument();
   607	            }
   608	            catch (BadInstallLocationKraken kraken)
   609	            {
   610	                // The folder exists and is not empty.
   611	                user.RaiseError("{0}", kraken.Message);
   612	                return badArgument();
   613	            }
   614	            catch (WrongGameVersionKraken kraken)
   615	            {
   616	                // Thrown because the specified game instance is too old for one of the selected DLCs.
   617	                user.RaiseError("{0}", kraken.Message);
   618	                return badArgument();
   619	            }
   620	            catch (NotGameDirKraken kraken)
   621	            {
   622	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceNotInstance, kraken.path);
   623	                return error();
   624	            }
   625	            catch (InvalidGameInstanceKraken)
   626	            {
   627	                // Thrown by Manager.SetAutoStart() if Manager.HasInstance returns false.
   628	                // Will be checked again down below with a proper error message
   629	            }
   630	
   631	            // Test if the instance was added to the registry.
   632	            // No need to test if valid, because this is done in AddInstance().
   633	            if (Manager.HasInstance(instanceName))
   634	            {
   635	                user.RaiseMessage(Properties.Resources.InstanceFakeDone);
   636	                return Exit.OK;
   637	            }
   638	            else
   639	            {
   640	                user.RaiseError(Properties.Resources.InstanceFakeFailed);
   641	                return error();
   642	            }
   643	        }
   644	
   645	        [ExcludeFromCodeCoverage]
   646	        private int UnknownCommand(string option)
   647	        {
   648	            user.RaiseError("{0}: instance {1}",
   649	                            Properties.Resources.UnknownCommand, option);
   650	            return Exit.BADOPT;
   651	        }
   652	
   653	        #endregion
   654	
   655	        [ExcludeFromCodeCoverage]
   656	        private void PrintUsage(string verb)
   657	        {
   658	            foreach (var h in InstanceSubOptions.GetHelp(verb))
   659	            {
   660	                user.RaiseError("{0}", h);
   661	            }
   662	        }

   665	    }
   666	}

3. `CloneInstance` now checks if `newPath` is a subdirectory of `existingInstance.GameDir`

Looking at `CloneGameInstanceDialog.buttonOK_Click` (lines 205-214):
```csharp

{

catch (Exception ex)
```

`PathErrorKraken` extends `Kraken`, so it will be caught by the first catch block and the error message will be displayed.

Now let me think about whether I should also fix the `CopyDirectory` issue more directly. Looking at the recursive call in `CopyDirectory`:

```csharp
foreach (var subdir in sourceDir.GetDirectories())
{
    var temppath = Path.Combine(destDirPath, subdir.Name);
    // ... 
    // Copy subdir contents to new location
    CopyDirectory(subdir.FullName, temppath, ...);
}
```

If `destDirPath` is a subdirectory of `sourceDirPath`, then when we iterate through `sourceDir.GetDirectories()`, the newly created `destDirPath` will appear as a subdirectory of `sourceDirPath`, and we'll try to copy it, creating a nested copy, and this will continue infinitely.

One alternative approach would be to skip the destination directory during the recursive copy. But that would be harder to implement correctly. The check in `CloneInstance` is sufficient.
